    <section class="article-seo gray-10">
    <div class="cmlabs-container">
                                    <h2 class="h2-700 h2-m-700">
    Content Writing Service - Optimize Your Website Visibility!
</h2>
<div class="main__written b1-400 b1-m-400 text-gray-100 d-flex align-items-center gap-2">
        <i class="bx bxs-user-circle"></i>
        <p class="m-0">
            Written by <span class="writter">cmlabs</span> July 08, 2024
        </p>
    </div>

<p class="p-400 p-m-400">
    According to Forbes, 90% of marketers regularly produce content as part of
    their marketing efforts, and content writing is one of them.
</p>
<p class="p-400 p-m-400">
    By regularly producing informative, relevant, and valuable articles,
    businesses can expand their reach, increase brand awareness, and achieve
    long-term success. However, the writing technique should not be done
    carelessly.
</p>
<a class="read-more-seo p-400 p-m-400 collapsed" data-bs-toggle="collapse" href="#readMoreCollapse" role="button" aria-expanded="false" aria-controls="collapseExample">Read more</a>
<div class="collapse" id="readMoreCollapse">
    <p class="p-400 p-m-400">
        Some businesses may need a content writing service to produce articles with
        the help of experienced experts.
    </p>
    <p class="p-400 p-m-400">
        Using a professional content writing service can also help businesses cut
        their resource budget because there is no need to recruit an in-house team
        or freelancers with questionable experience.
    </p>
    <p class="p-400 p-m-400">
        cmlabs is a reliable partner if you are looking for a Content Writing
        Service in both Indonesian and English.
    </p>
    <p class="p-400 p-m-400">
        Before finding out more about how cmlabs, as a professional content writing
        service, can help your business, read the following discussion thoroughly.
    </p>
    <h3 class="h3-700 h3-m-700">
        <a id="_81v5xhh3fly0"></a>What Are the Examples of High-Quality Content
        Writing?
    </h3>
    <p class="p-400 p-m-400">
        Everyone can write, but it is certainly not easy to present something
        high-quality and provide significant benefits to readers.
    </p>
    <p class="p-400 p-m-400">
        Meanwhile, to maximize brand awareness, for example, you need to present
        quality and relevant content.
    </p>
    <p class="p-400 p-m-400">
        So, what are examples of content writing that has reading value and can
        maximize business visibility in the online field? Every web content, whether
        it is an article or a blog, can be considered high quality if it has the
        following characteristics:
    </p>
    <h4 class="h4-700 h4-m-700"><a id="_raphxixln7qv"></a>1. Readable Content</h4>
    <p class="p-400 p-m-400">
        Content must be easy to read as readability is one of the main metrics that
        make high-quality content.
    </p>
    <p class="p-400 p-m-400">
        If a piece of writing is difficult to read, either because of a complicated
        sentence structure, the use of vocabulary that is not relevant to the
        reader's understanding, or because of an unattractive format, it will be
        difficult for the reader to understand the message to be conveyed.
    </p>
    <p class="p-400 p-m-400">
        Therefore, it is important to ensure that your blog posts are easy to read
        for a wide range of people, including general readers. If you subscribe to
        professional content writing services, then they will be given more focus on
        these matters:
    </p>
    <ul class="p-400 p-m-400">
        <li>
            <strong>Implementation of heading structure.</strong> The use of a
            hierarchy of headings or subheadings in content can help readers to
            understand the overall structure of the content.
        </li>
        <li>
            <strong>Use of sentence structure.</strong> To make your content easy to
            read, try to use short and clear sentences. You also need to avoid using
            sentences that are long, complicated, and potentially confusing to the
            reader.
        </li>
        <li>
            <strong>Produce articles in two languages:</strong> If your business
            operates in a global market or has an audience that speaks different
            languages, then you may need both English and Indonesian article writing
            services.
        </li>
        <li>
            <strong>User-friendly:</strong> Use words that the target reader
            understands and avoid technical terms that the reader may not be familiar
            with.
        </li>
    </ul>
    <h4 class="h4-700 h4-m-700">
        <a id="_udsrirq8wtea"></a>2. Understandable Content
    </h4>
    <p class="p-400 p-m-400">
        A high-quality article is an article that presents complete information and
        is easily understood by the target reader. Here are some things that must be
        considered to make an article easy to understand:
    </p>
    <ul class="p-400 p-m-400">
        <li>
            Organize the information in the article in a structured, systematic, and
            logical manner so that readers can follow the flow of thought easily.
        </li>
        <li>
            Avoid using overly technical terms or language that may be difficult for
            readers who are not experts in the field to understand.
        </li>
        <li>
            If the article discusses complex concepts or information, be sure to
            explain it clearly and simply. <strong>Tips:</strong> Use relevant
            examples or analogies to help readers understand the concept better.
        </li>
    </ul>
    <h4 class="h4-700 h4-m-700">
        <a id="_b0yppyj29znw"></a>3. Shareable Content
    </h4>
    <p class="p-400 p-m-400">
        One of the characteristics of a high-quality article is that it makes the
        reader want to share the news immediately after reading it.
    </p>
    <p class="p-400 p-m-400">
        If your article is successful in making readers want to share it, then this
        will be very beneficial because it will increase the organic reach of the
        content, including people outside of your immediate network.
    </p>
    <h4 class="h4-700 h4-m-700"><a id="_n3wjg1ip0teg"></a>4. Findable Content</h4>
    <p class="p-400 p-m-400">
        Findable refers to how easy it is for your target audience to find your
        content in search results. A high-quality article will generally be easier
        to find on search engines.
    </p>
    <p class="p-400 p-m-400">
        Generally, apart from writing informative and relevant content, you also
        need to implement SEO (Search Engine Optimization) strategies to make the
        article/blog easy to read by search engines.
    </p>
    <p class="p-400 p-m-400">
        Some of the main strategies that need to be done include:
    </p>
    <ul class="p-400 p-m-400">
        <li>Keyword research.</li>
        <li>Ensure the site structure is appropriate.</li>
        <li>Regular content optimization.</li>
        <li>Placement of keywords that are not excessive.</li>
        <li>Link-building, and many more.</li>
    </ul>
    <h4 class="h4-700 h4-m-700">
        <a id="_vz3zk8cwmrgn"></a>5. Memorable Content
    </h4>
    <p class="p-400 p-m-400">
        Many companies prefer to use the services of professional article writers
        because the writings produced are usually more memorable because they are
        executed directly by experts.
    </p>
    <p class="p-400 p-m-400">
        If readers find your high-quality content memorable, then when they search
        for other topics in your niche, they will likely choose your brand over
        competitors.
    </p>
    <p class="p-400 p-m-400">
        In addition, to make your articles memorable, you need to write content that
        is unique, original, and relevant to your readers' needs and interests.
    </p>
    <h3 class="h3-700 h3-m-700">
        <a id="_6k4m5aei3woa"></a>What Does a Content Writer Do to Optimize Website
        Visibility?
    </h3>
    <p class="p-400 p-m-400">
        One of the main goals of a content marketing strategy through article
        production is to optimize website visibility.
    </p>
    <p class="p-400 p-m-400">
        Here are tips for creating a high-quality online article to optimize website
        visibility:
    </p>
    <ul class="p-400 p-m-400">
        <li>
            Create a title (meta title) and description (meta description) that is
            interesting and relevant to the content of your article.
        </li>
        <li>
            Understand your target audience and what information they need from your
            website.
        </li>
        <li>Make sure your article can answer users' questions.</li>
        <li>
            Use heading tags (H1, H2, H3, etc.) strategically in the article to make
            it easier for readers and search engine bots to read and understand.
        </li>
        <li>
            Use internal links to direct readers to other pages on your website that
            are still relevant to the topic at hand.
        </li>
        <li>Make sure to regularly update the information in your articles.</li>
        <li>
            Do keyword research so that your articles can more easily appear in search
            results.
        </li>
    </ul>
    <p class="p-400 p-m-400">
        To make the results more significant, you can also apply SEO strategies when
        you create articles. If you are interested and want to learn more about the
        SEO Services package as well as Article Writing, please visit
        <span href="https://cmlabs.co/en-id/pricing/content-writing"><strong>SEO Content Writing Services by
                cmlabs</strong></span>.
    </p>
    <h3 class="h3-700 h3-m-700">

<script>
    function initializeCarousel(carouselId, duration = 50) {
        const carousel = document.getElementById(carouselId);
        if (carousel) {
            const carouselIndicators = carousel.querySelectorAll(".carousel-indicators button span");
            let intervalID;

            const reviewCarousel = new bootstrap.Carousel(carousel);

            window.addEventListener("load", function() {
                fillCarouselIndicator(1);
            });

            carousel.addEventListener("slide.bs.carousel", function(e) {
                let index = e.to;
                fillCarouselIndicator(++index);
            });

            function fillCarouselIndicator(index) {
                let i = 0;
                for (const carouselIndicator of carouselIndicators) {
                    if (carouselIndicator)
                        carouselIndicator.style.width = 0;
                }
                clearInterval(intervalID);
                reviewCarousel.pause();

                intervalID = setInterval(function() {
                    i++;

                    const spanLoader = carousel.querySelector(".carousel-indicators .active span")
                    if (spanLoader)
                        spanLoader.style.width = i + "%";


                    if (i >= 100)
                        reviewCarousel.next();

                }, duration);
            }
        }
    }
</script>

                            "X-CSRF-TOKEN": document
                                .querySelector('meta[name="csrf-token"]')
                                .getAttribute("content"),
                        },
                        method: "post",
                        body: JSON.stringify({
                            category: buttonDelete.getAttribute("data-category"),
                            type: buttonDelete.getAttribute("data-type"),
                            detail: buttonDelete.getAttribute("data-detail"),
                            locale: document
                                .getElementsByTagName("html")[0]
                                .getAttribute("lang"),
                            isDeleted: true,
                            region: "id",
                        }),
                    })
                    .then((response) => response.json())
                    .then((result) => {
                            const totallist = document.querySelector('#totallist')
                            const accordionlist = document.querySelector('#your-list');
                            const cartList = document.querySelector('.cart');
                            const totalCount = document.querySelector(`#total-${name}`);
                            const lists = document.querySelectorAll(`.card-list.${name}`).length;
                            const cartlist = document.querySelectorAll('.seos-lists').length;
                            const carttitle = document.querySelector('.cart-title');
                            const cardLists = document.querySelectorAll('.card-list').length;
                            const logincart = document.querySelector('.logins');
                            const totallists = document.querySelector('#total-lists');
                            const yourListContainer = document.querySelector(".your-list-container-writing");
                            const dividerContainer = document.querySelector(`.${name}-cart`);
                            const dividerContainerLength = document.querySelectorAll(`.${name}-cart`).length;
                            const cartTotal = document.querySelector(`.counter-${name}`);
                            const totalPricingCart = document.querySelector(".totalPricingCart");
                            let inputCheckedss = document.querySelectorAll(".form-check-input:checked");
                            const summaryList = document.querySelectorAll(".summary-container");
                            let btnSubmitList = document.getElementById("btn-submit-list");
                            const totalEstimation = document.querySelector("#total-estimation");
                            let emptyState = document.querySelector(".title-empty-state");
                            let summaryForm = document.getElementById('summary-form');
                            if (lists <= 1 && cardLists <= 1) {
                                cartList.classList.remove('d-none');
                                accordionlist.classList.add('d-none');
                                carttitle.classList.add('d-none');
                                logincart.classList.add('d-none');
                                totallist.classList.add('d-none');
                                totallists.classList.remove('d-lg-block');

                                                                $("#navbar-cart").hide()
                                $("#navbar-cart").removeClass("d-lg-flex")
                                                    }
                        totallist.innerHTML = '(' + (cardLists - 1) + ')'; totallists.innerHTML = (cardLists -
                            1); totalCount.innerHTML = "(" + (lists - 1) + ")"; buttonDelete.removeAttribute("disabled");
                        if (result.status == true) {
                            elmToastSuccess.querySelector(
                                ".message"
                            ).innerHTML = result.message;
                            elmToastSuccess.style.display = "block";
                            setTimeout(function() {
                                elmToastSuccess.style.display = "none";
                            }, 3000);

                            const buttonType = buttonDelete.dataset.type;
                            cardlist.forEach(cardList => {
                                if (cardList.classList.contains(buttonType)) {
                                    let parentCardList = cardList.parentElement;
                                    cardList.remove();
                                    if (parentCardList.innerHTML.trim() == '') {
                                        parentCardList.innerHTML =
                                            `<p class="no-list p-400 p-m-400 text-center text-dark-70 px-4">You don’t have any item order on your cart. Explore package <a href="https://cmlabs.co/en-id/pricing">here</a></p>`
                                    }
                                }
                            })
                            if (dividerContainerLength > 0) {
                                if (inputCheckedss.length <= 1) {
                                    summaryForm.style.display = "none";
                                    btnSubmitList.setAttribute("disabled", "");
                                    emptyState.style.display = "block";
                                }
                                const buttonType = buttonDelete.dataset.type;
                                summaryList.forEach(summary => {
                                    if (summary.classList.contains(buttonType)) {
                                        // const summaryParent = summary.parentElement;
                                        summary.remove();
                                        // summaryParent.remove();
                                    }
                                })
                                const writingDivider = dividerContainer.querySelectorAll(".list-divider");
                                const navCartDivider = yourListContainer.querySelectorAll(".list-divider");
                                if (writingDivider.length == 1) {
                                    dividerContainer.innerHTML =
                                        `<p class="text-center s-400 s-m-400 text-dark-40 px-4 no-list">You don’t have any item order on your cart. Explore package <a href="https://cmlabs.co/en-id/pricing">here</a></p>`
                                }
                                let totalArr = [];
                                let deletedArr = [];
                                inputCheckedss.forEach(input => {
                                    let costSelect = input.parentElement.parentElement.parentElement;
                                    let totalSelect = costSelect.querySelector('input[name=cost]').value;
                                    totalArr.push(totalSelect);
                                    const buttonType = buttonDelete.dataset.type;
                                    const inputValue = (input).value;
                                    if (inputValue.includes(buttonType)) {
                                        if (input.classList.contains("check-seo")) {
                                            const deletedCheckbox = input.parentElement.parentElement
                                                .parentElement;
                                            let costDeleted = deletedCheckbox.querySelector('input[name=cost]')
                                                .value;
                                            deletedArr.push(costDeleted)
                                        } else {
                                            const deletedCheckbox = input.parentElement.parentElement
                                                .parentElement;
                                            let costDeleted = deletedCheckbox.querySelector('input[name=cost]')
                                                .value;
                                            deletedArr.push(costDeleted)
                                        }
                                    }
                                })
                                const deletedNum = parseInt(deletedArr[0]);
                                const sum1 = parseInt(totalArr[0]);
                                const sum2 = parseInt(totalArr[1]);
                                const totalSum = sum1 + sum2;
                                const changeTotal = totalSum - deletedNum;
                                let estCosts = 0;

                                estCosts = parseInt(estCosts) + parseInt(changeTotal);
                                estCostLabel = changeTotal === 'Rp' ? estCosts.toString().replace(
                                    /\B(?=(\d{3})+(?!\d))/g, ".") : estCosts.toString().replace(
                                    /\B(?=(\d{3})+(?!\d))/g, ".");
                                totalEstimation.innerHTML = `Rp ${estCostLabel}`

                                writingDivider.forEach(devider => {
                                    if (writingDivider.length <= 4) {
                                        devider.remove();
                                    }
                                })
                                navCartDivider.forEach(divider => {
                                    if (navCartDivider.length <= 2) {
                                        divider.remove();
                                    }
                                })
                                cartTotal.innerHTML = "(" + (lists - 1) + ")";
                                totallist.innerHTML = "(" + ((cartlist / 2) - 1 + (lists / 2)) + ")";
                                totalCount.innerHTML = "(" + ((lists / 2) - 1) + ")";
                                totalPricingCart.innerHTML = ((cartlist / 2) - 1 + (lists / 2));
                                totallists.innerHTML = ((cartlist / 2) - 1 + (lists / 2));

                                if (((cartlist / 2) - 1 + (lists / 2)) == 0) {
                                    totallists.classList.remove("d-lg-block");
                                    cartList.classList.remove('d-none');
                                    accordionlist.classList.add('d-none');
                                    carttitle.classList.add('d-none');
                                    logincart.classList.add('d-none');
                                    totallist.classList.add('d-none');
                                    totallists.classList.remove('d-lg-block');
                                }
                            }

                            if (divider != null) {
                                divider.remove();
                            }

                            if (dividerContainerLength == 0) {
                                let parentCardList = cardList.parentElement;
                                cardList.remove();

                                if (divider != null) {
                                    divider.remove();
                                }
                                if (parentCardList.innerHTML.trim() == '') {
                                    parentCardList.parentElement.innerHTML =
                                        `<p class="text-center s-400 s-m-400 text-dark-40 px-4 no-list">You don’t have any item order on your cart. Explore package <a href="https://cmlabs.co/en-id/pricing/seo-services">here</a></p>`
                                }
                            }

                            let btnAddToList = document.querySelectorAll(
                                `.btn-add-to-list[data-category='${buttonDelete.getAttribute("data-category")}'][data-type='${buttonDelete.getAttribute("data-type")}']`
                            );

                            btnAddToList.forEach((btn) => {
                                btn.disabled = false;
                                btn.innerHTML = 'Add to cart';
                            })
                        } else {
                            elmToastError.querySelector(
                                ".message"
                            ).innerHTML = result.message;
                            elmToastError.style.display = "block";
                            setTimeout(function() {
                                elmToastError.style.display = "none";
                            }, 3000);
                        }
                    })
            .catch(function(error) {
                buttonDelete.removeAttribute("disabled");
                console.log(error);
            });
        }
    </script>

    <script>
        const navLinks = document.querySelectorAll('.nav-link.menu-item');

        // function to update icon class based on presence of .show class
        function updateIconClass(navLink) {
            const icon = navLink.querySelector('i[class*="bx"]');
            if (icon) {
                if (navLink.classList.contains('show')) {
                    const newClassNames = Array.from(icon.classList).map(className =>
                        className.startsWith('bx-') ? className.replace('bx-', 'bxs-') : className
                    );
                    icon.className = newClassNames.join(' ');
                } else {
                    const originalClassNames = Array.from(icon.classList).map(className =>
                        className.startsWith('bxs-') ? className.replace('bxs-', 'bx-') : className
                    );
                    icon.className = originalClassNames.join(' ');
                }
            }
        }

        navLinks.forEach(navLink => {
            const icon = navLink.querySelector('i[class*="bx-"]');

            if (icon) {
                navLink.addEventListener('mouseover', () => {
                    const newClassNames = Array.from(icon.classList).map(className =>
                        className.startsWith('bx-') ? className.replace('bx-', 'bxs-') : className
                    );
                    icon.className = newClassNames.join(' ');
                });

                navLink.addEventListener('mouseout', () => {
                    updateIconClass(navLink);
                });

                updateIconClass(navLink);

                const observer = new MutationObserver(mutations => {
                    mutations.forEach(mutation => {
                        if (mutation.attributeName === 'class') {
                            updateIconClass(navLink);
                        }
                    });
                });

                observer.observe(navLink, {
                    attributes: true,
                    attributeFilter: ['class']
                });
            }
        });
    </script>

                        ENGLISH_ID[0] :
                        BOTH_ID[0];
                });
                dataCostProfessional.forEach(data => {
                    data.dataset.cost = type === 'bahasa' ? BAHASA_ID[1] : type === 'english' ?
                        ENGLISH_ID[1] :
                        BOTH_ID[1];

                dataCostAdvanced.forEach(data => {
                    data.dataset.cost = type === 'bahasa' ? BAHASA_ID[2] : type === 'english' ?
                        ENGLISH_ID[2] :
                        BOTH_ID[2];
                });
            } else {

                        ENGLISH_EN[0] :
                        BOTH_EN[0];

    <script>
    const region = 'id';

    function ucfirst(str) {
        if (!str) return str;
        return str.charAt(0).toUpperCase() + str.slice(1);
    }

    <script>
        const fetchListData = (category = 'writing') => {
            fetch("/data/your-list", {
                    headers: {
                        "X-CSRF-TOKEN": document
                            .querySelector('meta[name="csrf-token"]')
                            .getAttribute("content"),
                    },
                    method: "get",
                })
                .then((response) => response.json())
                .then((result) => {
                    let yourListSeo = document.querySelectorAll("#your-list-seo-consultant .accordion-body");
                    let yourListWriting = document.querySelectorAll("#your-list-writing .accordion-body");
                    const isWritingServices = category.includes('writing') || category.includes('press-release') ||
                        category.includes('copywriting')
                    const serviceCountEl = isWritingServices ? document.querySelector("#total-writing") : document
                        .querySelector("#total-seo")

                    let yourListEl = isWritingServices ? yourListWriting : yourListSeo
                    let listCardResult = result.data.lists;

                    let isAuth = Object.prototype.toString.call(listCardResult) === '[object Array]';

                    yourListEl.forEach(elContainer => {
                        elContainer.innerHTML = `
                        <div class="card-list-group">
                            <div class="your-list-container d-flex flex-column gap-1">
                            </div>
                        </div>
                    `
                        let yourListContainer = elContainer.querySelector(".your-list-container");

                        listData = listCardResult;

                        const filteredItem = []

                        Object.keys(listData).forEach(key => {
                            const value = listData[key];
                            if (isWritingServices) {
                                if (key !== 'seo-services') {
                                    console.log('condition not same seo serv')
                                    if (value[region]) {
                                        let arr = Object.values(value[region]);
                                        let result = arr.map(item => JSON.parse(item));
                                        filteredItem.push(...result)
                                    }
                                }
                            } else {
                                if (key === 'seo-services') {
                                    if (value[region]) {
                                        let arr = Object.values(value[region]);
                                        let result = arr.map(item => JSON.parse(item));
                                        filteredItem.push(...result)
                                    }
                                }
                            }
                        });

                        serviceCountEl.innerHTML = `(${filteredItem.length})`

                        filteredItem.forEach((detail, idx) => {
                            // let detailData = JSON.parse(isAuth ? detail['detail'] : detail[1]);
                            let cardList = document.createElement("div");
                            let packageLanguage = detail.package.split("-")[1] ?? 'english'
                            let packageName = detail.package.split("-")[0]

                            switch (packageLanguage) {
                                case 'bahasa':
                                    packageLanguage = 'ID';
                                    break;
                                case 'english':
                                    packageLanguage = 'EN';
                                    break;
                                default:
                                    packageLanguage = 'en' === 'id' ? 'Both' :
                                        'Both';
                                    break;
                            }

                            cardList.className = "d-flex align-items-center card-list"
                            cardList.innerHTML = `
                            <div class="d-flex flex-column w-100">
                                <div class="d-flex flex-column">
                                    <p class='b2-400'>
                                        <span class="b2-400 b1-m-400 text-dark-70">${detail['label']} </span>
                                        <span class="b2-400 b1-m-400 text-dark-70"> - ${ucfirst(packageName) ?? ''}</span>
                                    </p>
                                </div>
                                <div class="d-flex flex-row gap-1">
                                    <small>${packageLanguage} - ${ucfirst(detail.country) ?? ''}</small>
                                </div>
                                <div class="d-flex flex-column">
                                    <div class="b2-400 b2-m-400 text-dark-70">Estimated Price</div>
                                    <div class="p-700 p-m-700 text-primary-70">${region === 'id' ? detail.cost['id_label'] : detail.cost['en_label'] }</div>
                                </div>
                            </div>
                            <button type="button" class="btn btn-w-icon btn-deletes" data-category="${category}" data-type="${detail['type']}" data-detail="${detail}">
                                <i class="bx bxs-x-circle btn-icon text-gray-110"></i>
                            </button>
                        `

                            let divider = document.createElement("div");
                            divider.className = 'list-divider';
                            const buttonDelete = cardList.querySelector("button");

                            yourListContainer.appendChild(cardList);

                            if (idx !== listData.length - 1)
                                yourListContainer.appendChild(divider);
                            else
                                divider = null;

                            buttonDelete.addEventListener("click", (e) => onDeleteListener(e,
                                buttonDelete, cardList, divider));

                        });
                    })
                    // update count on
                    const totalItems = $('.dropdown-cart-user .card-list').length

                    $('#total-lists').html(totalItems)
                    $('#totallist').html(`(${totalItems})`)
                });
        }
    </script>

    <script>
        document.addEventListener("DOMContentLoaded", function() {
            let menuSection = document.querySelectorAll('.cover-tab');
            let link = document.querySelectorAll('.cover-tab-link');

            // for clickable event
            menuSection.forEach(v => {
                v.onclick = (() => {
                    setTimeout(() => {
                        menuSection.forEach(j => j.classList.remove('active'))
                        v.classList.add('active')
                    }, 300)
                })
            })

            link.forEach(v => {
                v.onclick = (() => {
                    setTimeout(() => {
                        link.forEach(j => j.classList.remove('active'))
                        v.classList.add('active')
                    }, 300)
                })
            })

            // for window scrolldown event
            window.onscroll = function() {
                let mainSection = document.querySelectorAll('section');
                let link = document.querySelectorAll('.cover-tab-link');

                mainSection.forEach((v, i) => {
                    let rect = v.getBoundingClientRect().y
                    if (rect < window.innerHeight - 500) {
                        menuSection.forEach(v => v.classList.remove('active'))
                        menuSection[i].classList.add('active')
                        link.forEach(v => v.classList.remove('active'))
                        link[i].classList.add('active')
                    }
                })
            }
        })
    </script>

    <script>
        var x = window.matchMedia("(max-width: 767.98px)")
        myFunction(x)
        x.addListener(myFunction)

        function myFunction(x) {
            if (x.matches) { // If media query matches
                document.getElementById("langBtn").colSpan = "10";
                document.querySelectorAll('.nones').forEach(function(el) {
                    el.classList.add("hides");
                });
            } else {
                document.getElementById("langBtn").colSpan = "2";
                document.querySelectorAll('.nones').forEach(function(el) {
                    el.classList.remove("hides");
                });
            }
        }
    </script>

    <script>
        document.addEventListener("DOMContentLoaded", function() {
            const formInputs = document.querySelectorAll(".form-required-desktop");
            const submitButtons = document.querySelectorAll("#submitBtn");

            const formInputsMobile = document.querySelectorAll(".form-required-mobile");
            const submitButtonMobile = document.querySelectorAll("#submitBtnMobile");

            formInputs.forEach(function(input) {
                input.addEventListener("input", () => checkInputs(formInputs, submitButtons));
            });

            formInputsMobile.forEach(function(input) {
                input.addEventListener("input", () => checkInputs(formInputsMobile, submitButtonMobile));
            });

            function checkInputs(formInputs, submitButtons) {
                let empty = false;
                formInputs.forEach(function(input) {
                    if (input.value === '') {
                        empty = true;
                    }
                });

                if (empty) {
                    submitButtons.forEach((btn) => {
                        btn.disabled = true;
                    })
                } else {
                    submitButtons.forEach((btn) => {
                        btn.disabled = false;
                    })
                }
            }
        });
    </script>

        <script>
        function convertAndFillUSD() {
            const USD_EXCHANGE_RATE = document.getElementById("usd-idr-footer").value;

            const priceElements = document.querySelectorAll('.update-cost');

            priceElements.forEach(priceElement => {
                const idrValue = parseFloat(priceElement.getAttribute('data-cost'));
                const usdValue = (idrValue / USD_EXCHANGE_RATE);

                const formattedUSDValue = usdValue.toFixed(2);
                const usdValueWithoutDecimal = usdValue === Math.floor(usdValue) ? Math.floor(usdValue) :
                    formattedUSDValue;

                if ("id" == "id") {
                    priceElement.textContent = priceElement.getAttribute("data-id");
                } else {
                    var usdPrice = priceElement.getAttribute("data-usd")
                    if (usdPrice != "-") {
                        priceElement.textContent = usdPrice;
                    } else {
                        priceElement.textContent = "USD " + usdValueWithoutDecimal;
                    }
                }
            });
        }

        async function fetchExchangeRate() {
            try {
                const response = await fetch('https://currency-exchange.p.rapidapi.com/exchange?from=USD&to=IDR&q=1', {
                    method: 'GET',
                    headers: {
                        'X-RapidAPI-Key': '77fe18d216mshbe7bb1d4de0b02ap1553e1jsnb8c5add91843',
                        'X-RapidAPI-Host': 'currency-exchange.p.rapidapi.com'
                    }
                });
                const result = await response.text();
                document.getElementById("usd-idr-footer").value = result

                convertAndFillUSD()
            } catch (error) {
                console.error(error);
            }
        }

        fetchExchangeRate();
    </script>

        document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', function() {
            const floatingButtonContainer = document.querySelector('.mobile-menu');
            const floatingButtonContainerDesktop = document.querySelector('.floating-notification-section');
            const hiddFloatingMenu = document.querySelector('.hide-footer');

            function toggleFloatingButton() {
                const scrollPosition = window.scrollY;
                const hideFloatingMenuTop = hiddFloatingMenu.getBoundingClientRect().top +
                    scrollPosition - 100;
                const formTitleTop = formTitle.getBoundingClientRect().top + scrollPosition - 100;

                if (scrollPosition + window.innerHeight - 300 >= hideFloatingMenuTop) {
                    floatingButtonContainer.classList.add('d-none');
                    floatingButtonContainerDesktop.classList.add('d-none');
                } else {
                    floatingButtonContainer?.classList.remove('d-none');
                    floatingButtonContainerDesktop?.classList.remove('d-none');
                }
            }

            toggleFloatingButton();

            window.addEventListener('scroll', toggleFloatingButton);
        });

    <script>
        // Create cookie
        function setCookie(cname, cvalue, exdays) {
            const d = new Date();
            d.setTime(d.getTime() + (exdays * 24 * 60 * 60 * 1000));
            let expires = "expires=" + d.toUTCString();
            document.cookie = cname + "=" + cvalue + ";" + expires + ";path=/";
        }

        // Delete cookie
        function deleteCookie(cname) {
            const d = new Date();
            d.setTime(d.getTime() + (24 * 60 * 60 * 1000));
            let expires = "expires=" + d.toUTCString();
            document.cookie = cname + "=;" + expires + ";path=/";
        }

        // Read cookie
        function getCookie(cname) {
            let name = cname + "=";
            let decodedCookie = decodeURIComponent(document.cookie);
            let ca = decodedCookie.split(';');
            for (let i = 0; i < ca.length; i++) {
                let c = ca[i];
                while (c.charAt(0) == ' ') {
                    c = c.substring(1);
                }
                if (c.indexOf(name) == 0) {
                    return c.substring(name.length, c.length);
                }
            }
            return "";
        }

        function acceptCookieConsent() {
            deleteCookie('user_cookie_consent');
            setCookie('user_cookie_consent', 1, 30);
            document.getElementById("cookiesConsentCard").remove();
        }

        (function() {
            const menu = document.getElementById("navbar-logo")
            const notif = document.getElementById("cookiesConsentCard")
            const dissmissBtn = document.querySelector("#cookiesConsentCard .reject-button")
            const confirmButton = document.querySelector("#cookiesConsentCard .confirm-button")

            Popper.createPopper(menu, notif, {
                placement: 'bottom-start',
                strategy: 'fixed',
                modifiers: [{
                        name: 'arrow',
                        options: {
                            padding: 12
                        },
                    },
                    {
                        name: 'offset',
                        options: {
                            offset: [0, 2],
                        },
                    },
                ],
            });

            dissmissBtn.addEventListener("click", () => {
                notif.remove()
            })

            confirmButton.addEventListener("click", () => {
                acceptCookieConsent()
                notif.remove()
            })
        })()
    </script>
    <script>
